(1) ORCH-0667 step 7c — field-shape skip. (2) Cycle-1 IMPL STEP X assumed prop pass-through. (3) Cycle-2 spec assumed feedback channel visibility. > **2026-04-23 night — AH-186 ORCH-0640.R-01 REGRESSION DISPATCHED. Device smoke step 1 FAILED.** User device test of T-27 (swipe right to save) showed "Already saved" alert for a card user never saved. Orchestrator investigated: root cause is legacy pre-save existence check at `app-mobile/src/components/AppHandlers.tsx:695-728` — pre-ORCH-0640 duplicate guard that queries `saved_card` and alerts if any row matches `(profile_id, experience_id=card.id)`. Post-cutover, `card.id` on the deck is a `place_pool.id`; stale saved_card rows from pre-ORCH-0640 sometimes have `experience_id` coincidentally matching, producing false positives. `savedCardsService.saveCard` already uses `upsert(onConflict='profile_id,experience_id')` against the verified-live unique index `saved_card_profile_experience_idx` — so the pre-save check is redundant AND actively harmful. **Fix: delete the 34-line block.** Upsert handles duplicates idempotently (overwrites card_data, refreshing stale display state on re-swipe). Curated cards already bypass this check and work correctly — proves the delete is safe. **Prompt:** `prompts/IMPL_ORCH-0640_R_01_ALREADY_SAVED_FALSE_POSITIVE.md`. **Scope: ONE file, ONE block delete.** No DB migration. No edge fn deploy. Mobile OTA only after approval. **ORCH-0640 status rolled back from CONDITIONAL_CLOSED to REGRESSION_IN_FLIGHT.** Retest cycle counter now 2 of 2 — this is the last rework before escalation. **Trigger:** user report "1. Fail. Says the card is already saved when it is not."

## Historical (Pre-Orchestrator)

Extensive investigation, spec, implementation, and test work was completed across 10+ deck hardening passes, full card pipeline audit (5 passes), notification system audit (2 passes), and multiple targeted fix cycles. See LAUNCH_READINESS_TRACKER.md for the full evidence chain.
